\hypertarget{group__Quadratures}{}\doxysection{Quadratures}
\label{group__Quadratures}\index{Quadratures@{Quadratures}}


Classes providing quadratures rules on cells, faces and edges, as well as cost-\/effective ways to compute Gram matrices of polynomial bases.

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Classes providing quadratures rules on cells, faces and edges, as well as cost-\/effective ways to compute Gram matrices of polynomial bases.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GMGolyCompl()}{GMGolyCompl()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Eigen\+::\+Matrix\+Xd H\+Ar\+D\+Core3\+D\+::\+G\+M\+Goly\+Compl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Cell \&}]{T,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classHArDCore3D_1_1GolyComplBasisCell}{Goly\+Compl\+Basis\+Cell}} \&}]{basis1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classHArDCore3D_1_1GolyComplBasisCell}{Goly\+Compl\+Basis\+Cell}} \&}]{basis2,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{s1,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{s2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__Quadratures_ga3d20f8d4cc0e064972c1e74f65e468d2}{Monomial\+Integrals\+Type}}}]{mono\+\_\+int\+\_\+map,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{m1 = {\ttfamily 3},  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{m2 = {\ttfamily 3},  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{k1 = {\ttfamily 3},  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{k2 = {\ttfamily 3} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the Gram Matrix of the (optionally k1th derivative of the) s1th section of Goly\+Compl (optionally multiplied by the m1th variable) and the (optionally k2th derivative of the) s2th section of Goly\+Compl (optionally multiplied by the m2th variable) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em T} & Cell to which the basis corresponds \\
\hline
{\em basis1} & First basis \\
\hline
{\em basis2} & Second basis \\
\hline
{\em s1} & the first Goly\+Compl basis has three sections; use the s1th. \\
\hline
{\em s2} & the second Goly\+Compl basis has three sections; use the s2th. \\
\hline
{\em mono\+\_\+int\+\_\+map} & list of integrals of monomials up to the sum of max degree of basis1 and basis2 \\
\hline
{\em m1} & Optionally (m1 $<$ 3), add one to the power of the m1th variable \\
\hline
{\em m2} & Optionally (m2 $<$ 3), add one to the power of the m2th variable \\
\hline
{\em k1} & Optionally (k1 $<$ 3), take the k1th derivative of the first Goly\+Compl scalar \\
\hline
{\em k2} & Optionally (k2 $<$ 3), take the k2th derivative of the second Goly\+Compl scalar \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__Quadratures_gac20dbc474166b1b7412c65d48cabb68c}\label{group__Quadratures_gac20dbc474166b1b7412c65d48cabb68c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Quad\+Rule\+Tetra\+::\+Quad\+Rule\+Tetra (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{doe,  }\item[{bool}]{warn }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create a quadrature rule with at least the given degree of exactness (if available). 

The smallest such quadrature rule will be chosen. If none are available, the highest degree available will be used. \mbox{\Hypertarget{group__Quadratures_ga0d95447bb72cfc1b19cd2ea192ff6695}\label{group__Quadratures_ga0d95447bb72cfc1b19cd2ea192ff6695}}
